name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom - Garden-View (Double bed)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:18 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:First of all, the overall hotel is good, the service is very enthusiastic, and there is a shuttle bus to Nishan Holy Land, which is very convenient. The hotel room is relatively clean, and the breakfast is especially good, with many local specialties.
Although the hotel environment is okay, considering that the selling point here is the environment of mountains and rivers, it can't be considered very good. There are small bridges, flowing water, flowers, plants and trees, but the exquisiteness is average, and it is relatively small. It is only a little over 1 kilometer to walk around. Compared with similar hotels or homestays, it is not outstanding.
Let's talk about Nishan Holy Land. We decided to come here after reading the guide. It can only be said that it is okay, and if you don't bring children, there is no need to come. The natural scenery is at the level of a suburban park in a big city. As for culture and study, it is relatively rough. The study activity of 368 yuan per hour is actually the tour guide's explanation, and there are not many knowledge points. The cost performance is really low. The only highlight is the fireworks show, but it seems that it is not meaningful to come just to watch the fireworks for a few minutes.
So in summary, I think Nishan Holy Land itself is not worth coming, but if you must come, this hotel is a very good choice. Just don't regard the hotel as the main part of enjoying the vacation, and don't have too high expectations for the environment.
